        select distinct codclien  from Mconsultas where fecha_cita between '09/01/2018' and '09/01/2018'and asistido=3   and codmedico= s.codmedico 
    )
    
    ) AS decimal )/COUNT( distinct P.codclien )  efectividad
    from Mconsultas P
    inner join Mmedicos m On m.Codmedico=P.codmedico
    where P.fecha_cita between '09/01/2018' and '09/01/2018' and asistido=3 
    GROUP BY P.codmedico order by efectividad desc
